 vaise chidambaram ke baad saal 2013 main tatkaaleen grih mantri susheel kumaar scindia ne bhi ensitisi ke gathan ke prastaav par rajyon ke bich sahmati kaayam karne kii koshish kii thi lekin kamyaabi nahin mil saki
 a senior official says, "the proposal will include the entire process of collecting, examining and taking action on intelligence received from various sources under the NCTC at one place
" ' unke mutabiq prastaavit ensitisi ko sidhe grih mantralay ke maatahat karne kii baat shaamil hogi
 The previous proposal included a proposal to set it up under the Intelligence Bureau ie IB
 darasal rajya sarkaron ko ibi par bharosa he isliye wo iskaa virodh kar rahi hai

 sutron ke anusaar pichley saal oktober main chidambaram kii adhyakshata vaali sansad kii sthaayee samiti ne grih sachiv rajeev maharishi se ensitisi ke bhavishya ko lekar sarkaar kii yojana ke bare main poochtacha kii thi

 supreme court ne buudhvaar ko chunaav ayog main niyukti ko lekar sakht tippanee kii he

 court ne apni tippanee main kaha ki abhi tak sabhi niyuktiyaan nishpaksh or sahi dhang se hui hai lekin hamen lagata he ki iske liye koi tay prakriya nahin he
 a petition was filed in the Supreme Court for appointment to the Election Commission, demanding the constitution of a constitutional panel comprising the Leader of the Opposition and the Chief Justice for the appointment of Election Commissioners
 jisaki sunwaayee ke dauraan court ne centre sarkaar ko sakht hidaayat di he ki atorni general se poocha he kikya sikret ballat ke jariye niyuktiki ja sakati he
 The court has asked the Attorney General to clear the situation in the case
 chunaav ayog main niyuktiyon ko lekar sawaal uthte rahe hai
 cecs and commissioners are usually appointed on the basis of seniority
 lekin kai baar is prakriya ko lekar sawaal bhi khadey hue hai

 raashtrapati pranab mukherjee ne jyoti kii niyukti ko manjuuri de di he
 He will take over on July 6

 munde samarthakon ne unki maut kii sibiai jaanch kii maang ko lekar kendriya grahamantri rajnath singh or bijepi ke varisht netaa laalkrishna adwani kii gadiyon ko rokane kii koshish kii
 It is being told that some vehicles were set on fire and some vehicles were also pelted with stones
 mukhyamantri prithviraj chavaan kii gaadi par bhi patharav kiya gaya
 There are reports of injuries to some policemen and some common people in this uproar
 kadi dhoop main apane priy netaa ko antim vidaai dene ai dukh se sarabor kshetra kii janata munde kii antim jhalak paane ke liye aatur thi or is kram main unki naaraazgi bhi saamne ai
 At the funeral site, Munde supporters started throwing stones at the police party, after which the police had to lathi-charge
 iske baad unki putree pankaja ne manch par aage aakar naaraaz sthaneey logon se shant rahane or vyavastha banaaye rakhane kii apil kii
 However, the situation deteriorated once again when people demanded a CBI inquiry into Munde's death and broke after the last rites 
 bheed ne ek car main aag laga di or mukhyamantri prithviraj chavaan evam kuch anya mantriyon ke vaahan kaa maarg baadhit kar diya

 hariyaali teej sawan maheene ke shuklapaksh kii tritiya tithi ko manaayi jaati he
 This beloved festival of women of North India is not only a religious festival but also a day to celebrate nature
 is parv ko shrawani teej yaa kajri teej bhi kehete hai
 This year it is falling on Wednesday i
e
 26 July
 barish ke is mausam main van-upavan, khet aadi hariyaali kii chadar se lipte hote hai
 The entire nature satisfies the mind with a panoramic view of green
 isliye sawan maheene kaa yah tyohaar hariyaali teej kehalaata he
 According to mythological rituals, Goddess Parvati had undergone hard penance for a hundred years to attain Mahadev Shiva
 apni athak sadhana se unhone isi din bhagwaan shiv ko praapt kiya tha
 This is the reason why married women keep this fast in order to achieve their happy married life and unbroken good fortune
 parampara ke anusaar yogya var kii prapti ke liye kunvaari kanyaayein bhi yah vrath rakhti hai
 Henna, Jhula and Suhaag-mark Singhare have special importance in this festival of Hariyali Teej
 striyaan menhadi, jo ki suhaag kaa pratik he, se haathon ko sajaati hai
 Swings are carried out from place to place in villages and towns
 kajri geet gaati hui mahilaayein samuhik rup se jhula jhulati hai
 On this special occasion, there is a tradition of inviting newlyweds from their in-laws
 ve apane saath singhara laati he
 Also the in-laws are sent clothes, jewelry, suhaag items, sweets and henna, which is considered as Teej's offering
 tippaniyan Mata Parvati rides are taken out in many places with great pomp and grand fair is organized
 aise melon main jaipur main yojit hone vaala teej mata utsav vishesh darshneey he
 Here the idol of Goddess Parvati, called Teej Mata, has been worshiped since the time of the raja-rajvadas
 jaipur ke teej juluus main teej mata parvati kii ek jhalak paane or darshan ke liye dur-dur se shraddhalu aate hai
 In this rainy season, the forest groves, fields etc
 are wrapped with a sheet of greenery
 sampurna prakruti hare rang ke manoram drishy se man ko trupt karti he
 Therefore, this festival of Sawan month is called Hariyali Teej
 puranic anushrutiyon ke anusaar, devi parvati ne mahadev shiv ko praapt karne ke liye sau varshon tak kathin tapasya kii thi
 He received Lord Shiva on this day by his tireless practice
 yahi kaaran he ki vivaahit mahilaayein apane sukhmay vivaahit jivan or akhand saubhaahgya kii prapti liye yah vrath rakhti hai
 According to tradition, virgin girls also keep this fast to get a worthy bride
 hariyaali teej ke is parv main menhadi, jhula or suhaag-chihn singhare kaa vishesh mahatv he
 Women decorate their hands with henna, a symbol of honey
 gaanv-kasbon main jagah-jagah jhule lagaae jate hai
 The women sing the Kajari song, swinging collectively
 is vishesh avasar par navvivaahitaaon ko unke sasuraal se maayke bulaane kii parampara he
 She brings Singhara with her
 saath hi sasuraal se kapade, gahane, suhaag kaa saamaan, mithai or menhadi bheji jaati he, jise teej kaa bhent mana jaataa he
 The comments anek sthanon par bade dhoomdhaam se mata parvati kii sawari nikaali jaati he or bhavy meley kaa aayojan hota he
 The Teej Mata Utsav held in Jaipur at such fairs is special
 yahaan devi parvati kii pratimaa, jinhen teej mata kaha jaataa he, kii puja raja-rajavaadon ke samay se hoti aa rahi he

 telugana ke vakeelon kii sanyukt karrwai samiti ne jagan kii bhukh hadtaal main baadha daalane kii dhamkee di he
 On the other hand, state ministers and Congress mlas announced not to resign so that they could vote against the resolution on Telangana in the assembly
 mantriyon or vidhayakon sahit congress ke 70 se zyada vidhayakon evam netaaon ne mukhyamantri en
 Decided in a meeting with Kiran Kumar Reddy
 netaaon ne andhra pradesh ke vibhaajan kaa virodh karne kii thaanee he
 In protest against the bifurcation of Andhra Pradesh, protesters took to the streets and forcibly closed hotels and shops
 virodh main mukhya margo par pahie phunke gaye
 They blocked state roads and national stateways, blocking traffic from Karnataka, Tamil Nadu and Odisha
 kahin-kahin se hinsa kii bhi jaankaree mili he
 The protesters burnt effigies of Congress leaders and shouted 'jai Samaikya Andhra' and brought to a standstill the lives of Visakhapatnam, Vijayawada, Guntur, Tirupati, Anantapur, Kurnool and other cities
 vijayangaram main congress ke pradesh adhyaksh botsa satyanarayan ke camp karyaalay par hamalaa bolne vaali bheed ko teetar-bitar karne ke lae police ne aansu gas kaa prayog kiya
 The protesters have sat on a sit-in near Botsa's office here
 vijaywada or vishakhapattanam main bijli utpaadan tham gaya he kyonki yahaan ke karmchaaree 48 ghanton ke band main shaamil ho gaye hai
 Officials have said that this will adversely affect the power supply in some districts
 anantpur or prakasham jile main bhi tanaav paidaa ho gaya
 The Telugu Desam Party and YSR Congress workers clashed here
 telugana ke virodh main karmchaariyon kii hadtaal ke kaaran kareeb do maah se sarkari swaamitv vaali basen nahin chal rahi hai

 saath hi aatankwaad ko lekar pakistan ko kathghare main khadaa kiya
 Meanwhile, PM Modi also targeted political parties questioning the action of security forces and seeking evidence
 bhartiya vayusena ke wing commander abhinandan kaa zikr karte hue modi ne kaha ki jaanbaaj air warrior abhinandan bhi tamilnadu se aate hai
 Every Indian is proud to be a Wing Commander
 aapako bataa den ki buudhvaar ko bhartiya payalat abhinandan ko pakistan ne pakad liya tha
 However, later on Thursday, Pakistani PM Imran Khan announced to leave Abhinandan
 wing commander abhinandan ko apana celut, sandesh yahaan post kareniske alaava piem modi ne yah bhi kaha ki desh kii pehali mahila rakshaamantri nirmala sitaraman bhi tamilnadu se aati hai, jinke netritv main bhartiya sena aage bad rahi he
 The PM said that India has been battling terrorism for many years
 ab aatankwaad ke masale par bharat asahaay nahin hai
 Between 2004 and 2014, there were many terrorist attacks in India
 desh ko ummid thi ki aatankwaadiyon ko unke karatuut kii sajaa milegi, lekin kabhi kuch nahin hua
 Targeting Pakistan, PM Modi said that India was expecting action against the terrorists of 26 / 11 Mumbai attack, but nothing happened
 pakistan ko iske saboot bhi die gaye, lekin usne koi karrwai nahin kii
 The news of the then Indian Army taking action against Pakistan also came to the media, but it was stopped
 piem modi ne raily ko sambodhit karte hue kaha ki hamaari sarkaar ke samay main uri main sena par aatanki hamalaa hua, jiske baad aap sabhi ne dekha he ki kya hua he
 Let me tell you that after the Uri terror attack, India entered into a surgical strike in Pakistan Occupied Kashmir and destroyed the terrorists' bases
 isamen kaaphi sankhya main aatankwaadi bhi maare gaye the
 Even after this action, Pakistan did not desist from its action and a terrorist attack was carried out in Pulwama, in which 40 CRPF personnel were killed
 is ghatana ke baad bharat ne pakistan main ghuskar air strike kii or aatanki sanghathan jaish-e-mohammad ke thikaanon ko tabah kar diya
 Everyone has seen this bravery of the Indian Army
 piem modi ne kaha, 'desh kii seva main ji jaan lagane vaale sabhi bahadur sainikon ko main salaam karata hum
 Due to their vigilance, our country is safe
 is avasar par piem modi ne sabase tej chalane vaali train tejas ko hari jhandi dikhaai
 This train will run between Madurai to Chennai
 saath hi rameswaram se dhanushkodi ke bich railway line kii neenv bhi rakhi gai
 Laying the foundation of the railway line, PM Modi said that this railway line was damaged after the disaster of 1964
 itnaa samay biit jane ke baavjood isko durust karne kii ore tanik bhi dhyaan nahin diya gaya tha
 He said that under the PM Kisan Yojana, the first installment has been sent to the account of one crore 10 lakh farmers
 unhone logon ko sambodhit karte hue kaha ki jaraa sochie ki ek farvari ko jis yojana kii ghoshnaa kii gai, usko usee maheene lagu kar diya gaya
 We worked 24 hours non-stop to implement this scheme in 24 days
 piem modi ne kaha ki 30 saal baad 2014 main pehali baar kisi party ne bahumat ke saath sarkaar banaai
 Through this, people gave a clear message that they want a strong government, which can take tough decisions
 piem ne kaha ki log eemaandaaree chaahate hai, vanshavaad nahin
 People want development, not destruction
 log unnati chaahate hai, policy paralisis nahin
 People want opportunities, not barriers
 log suraksha chaahate hai, gatirodh nahin
 People want integrated growth, not vote bank politics
 is dauraan piem modi ne bhartiya machuaaron kii aay main ijapha karne kii baat bhi kahi
 He said that if we want to increase the income of fisherman brothers and sisters, then we have to develop the infrastructure related to fisheries
 unhone kaha ki bharat sarkaar machuaaron kii suraksha or behatari ke liye samvedansheel he
 Since May 2014, hundreds of fishermen have been rescued from Sri Lanka due to diplomatic efforts
 iske alaava piem modi ne andhra pradesh ke vishakhapatnam main bhi ek raily ko sambodhit kiya
 During this, he attacked the Chief Minister of the state, Chandrababu Naidu
 naidu kaa naam liye bina modi ne kaha ki agar yahaan ke netaa apana kaam eemaandaaree se kiya hota, to unako apni naakaami kaa thikra modi par nahin phodna padataa
 During this, he said that some people have a challenge to save their political existence, for which they are lying day and night
 sangam vihaar main ek dil dahala dene vaali ghatana saamne ai he
 a 50-year-old freak tried to burn five girl children in the neighborhood
 vakt rahete police ne aasapaas ke logon kii madad se paanchon bacchiyon ko bachaa liya
 According to the news, accused Bharat Bhushan called five girls of the neighborhood to his home on the pretext of Kanya Poojan
 usne pehle ladakiyon ko khilaayaa pilaayaa, lekin jab ladakiyon ne ghar jane kii baat kahi to usne darwaja band kar diya or gas kii pipe kaat di
 After this he put kerosene on the girls and the floor
 tab tak bacchon ke maa baap unhen talashte hue bharat bhushan ke ghar ke baahar pahunch chuke the
 Bharat Bhushan started threatening with a match in his hand that he would burn the five girls
 logon ne police ko phone karke isaki jaankaree di
 Police reached the spot and tried to convince him
 ehtiyaat ke daur par kamare main pani daalane kaa intjaam kar liya gaya
 Neighbors drove a water motor and wet sheets were placed outside the house so that these sheets could be put on the children in case of fire
 iske baad police ne ek bada pathar markar darwaja khol diya or paanchon bacchiyon ko sahi salaamat baahar nikaal liya gaya
 It is said that Bharat Bhushan's daughter-in-law filed a dowry case against her family
 is silsile main uske parivaar ke kuch logon kii giraftaar bhi ho chuki he
 Angry about this, Bharat Bhushan got into the craze of burning girls
 uskaa kahana he ki ye bacchiyaan bhi aage chalakar bahu banengi or kisi kaa ghar barbaad karengi
 So he wanted to kill these girls by burning them
 ruthik roshan kii aagaamee film 'kaabil' kaa nayaa gaanaa 'sara jamaana' abhinetri urvashi rotela par filmaaya gaya he
 In this song, Urvashi has won the hearts of the audience with her superb dance and that is why both Urvashi and her song are trending on the internet
 is gane ko raftaar or paayal dev ne gaaya he, jabaki original 'sara jamaana' gane ko kishor kumaar ne gaaya tha
 This song was from Amitabh Bachchan's film 'yarana'
 yah he 'kaabil' kaa nayaa gaanaa 'haseenon kaa divaana'-agar 'haseenon kaa divaana' pasand nahin aayaa, to dekhie 'sara jamaana'-tippaniyan Let me tell you, the song 'sara Jamana' of Amitabh Bachchan's film 'yarana' has been a tremendous hit in its era
